\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900 \textcolor{keyword}{def }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesonic__cli__bgp_a5b886e9028afa3730c2c01edf791d8ae}{seconds\_to\_dhms\_str}}(seconds):}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901     sec = int(seconds)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902     hours = int(sec)/(60*60)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903     sec \%= (60*60)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1904     minutes = sec/60}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905     sec \%= 60}

\DoxyCodeLine{1881 \textcolor{keyword}{def }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesonic__cli__bgp_a5e159defc7bea70b69923d0df12e0708}{seconds\_to\_wdhm\_str}}(seconds):}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882     d = datetime.now()}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883     d = d -\/ timedelta(seconds=int(seconds))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884     weeks = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885     days = d.day  }
\DoxyCodeLine{1886     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} days != 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1887        days = days -\/ 1 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1888        \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} days != 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889           weeks = days // 7}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890           days = days \% 7}
\DoxyCodeLine{1891     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} weeks != 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1892         wdhm = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\{\}w\{\}d\{:02\}h'}.format(int(weeks), int(days), int(d.hour))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893     \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} days != 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894         wdhm = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\{\}d\{:02\}h\{:02\}m'}.format(int(days), int(d.hour), int(d.minute))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896         wdhm = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\{:02\}:\{:02\}:\{:02\}'}.format(int(d.hour), int(d.minute), int(d.second))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897 }
